
CREATE TABLE GMUT5000 (
       TIP_KOD VARCHAR(5) NOT NULL,
       TIP_ACIKLAMA VARCHAR(20) NOT NULL,
       TIP_SEVIYE INTEGER DEFAULT 1 NOT NULL,
       TIP_GROUP VARCHAR(1) default 'T' NOT NULL,
       REF_TIP VARCHAR(5),
       SABIT INTEGER default 0 NOT NULL
);


/* Table: GMUT5001  */
CREATE TABLE GMUT5001 (
       ID INTEGER DEFAULT 0 NOT NULL,
       TIP_KOD VARCHAR(5) NOT NULL,
       MASTERID INTEGER,
       KOD VARCHAR(25) NOT NULL,
       FULL_KOD VARCHAR(25) NOT NULL,
       ACK VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,
       SECIM INTEGER DEFAULT 1 NOT NULL,
       SEVIYE INTEGER DEFAULT 0 NOT NULL,
       DUMMY INTEGER DEFAULT 0 NOT NULL,
       EK_KOD VARCHAR(10),
       SABIT INTEGER default 0 NOT NULL,
      CONSTRAINT UQ_GMUT5001 UNIQUE (TIP_KOD,FULL_KOD)
);


CREATE TABLE GMUT5002 (
       ID INTEGER NOT NULL,
       REF_ID INTEGER NOT NULL,
      CONSTRAINT PK_GMUT5002 PRIMARY KEY (ID,REF_ID)
);

/* Table: GMUT5004  */
CREATE TABLE GMUT5004 (
       ID INTEGER NOT NULL,
       REF_ID INTEGER NOT NULL,
       PAR_KOD VARCHAR(12) NOT NULL,
       ANSWER INTEGER
);

/* Table: GMUT5005  */
CREATE TABLE GMUT5005 (
       PAR_KOD VARCHAR(12) NOT NULL,
       TIP_KOD VARCHAR(5) NOT NULL,
       PAR_TYPE INTEGER DEFAULT 0 NOT NULL,
       ACK VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL
);

/* Table: GMUT5006  */
CREATE TABLE GMUT5006 (
       ID INTEGER NOT NULL,
       PAR_KOD VARCHAR(12) NOT NULL,
       ANSWER VARCHAR(20)
);

/*  Check Constraints  */
COMMIT WORK;
